<script>
    window.loadjs = window.loadjs || function (url, callback, async) {
        async = typeof async === "undefined" ? true : async;
        var script = document.createElement("script");

        function onload() {
            var readyState = script.readyState;
            if (typeof readyState == "undefined" || /^(loaded|complete)$/.test(readyState)) {
                script.onload = script.onreadystatechange = null;
                script = null;
                callback && callback();
            }
        }

        script.async = async;
        if (script.readyState) {
            script.onreadystatechange = onload;
        } else {
            script.onload = onload;
        }
        script.src = url;
        var parent = document.getElementsByTagName("body")[0] || document.body;
        parent.appendChild(script) && (parent = null);
    }


    if (window.asyncJsList && window.asyncJsList instanceof Array) {
        window.asyncJsList.push(
                'https://j1.58cdn.com.cn/resource/xxzl/public/index_v0.js',//右侧工具栏返回顶部
                'https://j1.58cdn.com.cn/webim/js/entry_v20200420115253.js',
                "https://tracklog.58.com/referrer4.js"
        )
    } else {
        window.asyncJsList = [
            'https://j1.58cdn.com.cn/resource/xxzl/public/index_v0.js',
            'https://j1.58cdn.com.cn/webim/js/entry_v20200420115253.js',
            "https://tracklog.58.com/referrer4.js"];
    }

    window.onload = function () {
        var list = window.asyncJsList;
        if (list && list instanceof Array) {
            for (var i = 0; i < list.length; i++) {
                loadjs(list[i]);
            }
        }
    }
</script>
